  @delta_P(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @delta_P_0(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @delta_P_1(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @delta_P_2(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @delta_P_3(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @delta_P_4(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @delta_P_5(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @delta_P_6(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @delta_P_7(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @new_P(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @new_P_0(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @new_P_1(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @new_P_2(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @new_P_3(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @new_P_4(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @new_P_5(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @new_P_6(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  @new_P_7(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  E(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  E_0(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  E_1(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  E_2(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  E_3(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  E_4(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  E_5(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  E_6(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  E_7(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  P(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  P_0(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  P_1(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  P_2(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  P_3(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  P_4(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  P_5(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  P_6(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
  P_7(a:i:number,b:i:number) 
 END DECLARATION
 BEGIN MAIN
  BEGIN_STRATUM 0
   LOAD DATA FOR E FROM {{{"","default"},{"IO","file"},{"directory","facts"},{"extension",".facts"},{"filename","facts/E.facts"},{"location","fact-dir"},{"name","E"},{"stratum","slave"}}[{{"","default"},{"IO","file"},{"directory","facts"},{"extension",".facts"},{"filename","facts/E.facts"},{"location","fact-dir"},{"name","E"},{"stratum","slave"}}]}
  END_STRATUM 0
  BEGIN_STRATUM 1
   BEGIN_DEBUG "E_0(a,b) :- \n   E(a,b),\n   (a%8) = 0.\nin file /home/default/souffle/experiments/NR-splitjoin-8-first.dl [6:1-6:31]"
    QUERY
     IF (NOT (E = ∅))
      FOR t0 IN E
       IF ((t0.0%number(8)) = number(0))
        PROJECT (t0.0, t0.1) INTO E_0
   END_DEBUG
  END_STRATUM 1
  BEGIN_STRATUM 9
   BEGIN_DEBUG "P_0(a,b) :- \n   E_0(a,b).\nin file /home/default/souffle/experiments/NR-splitjoin-8-first.dl [8:1-8:22]"
    QUERY
     IF (NOT (E_0 = ∅))
      FOR t0 IN E_0
       PROJECT (t0.0, t0.1) INTO P_0
   END_DEBUG
   QUERY
    FOR t0 IN P_0
     PROJECT (t0.0, t0.1) INTO @delta_P_0
   LOOP
    PARALLEL
     BEGIN_DEBUG "P_0(a,b) :- \n   P_0(a,x),\n   P_0(x,b).\nin file /home/default/souffle/experiments/NR-splitjoin-8-first.dl [8:23-8:54]"
      QUERY
       IF ((NOT (@delta_P_0 = ∅)) AND (NOT (P_0 = ∅)))
        FOR t0 IN @delta_P_0
         FOR t1 IN P_0 ON INDEX t1.a = t0.1
          IF ((NOT (t0.1,t1.1) ∈ @delta_P_0) AND (NOT (t0.0,t1.1) ∈ P_0))
           PROJECT (t0.0, t1.1) INTO @new_P_0
     END_DEBUG
     BEGIN_DEBUG "P_0(a,b) :- \n   P_0(a,x),\n   P_0(x,b).\nin file /home/default/souffle/experiments/NR-splitjoin-8-first.dl [8:23-8:54]"
      QUERY
       IF ((NOT (P_0 = ∅)) AND (NOT (@delta_P_0 = ∅)))
        FOR t0 IN P_0
         FOR t1 IN @delta_P_0 ON INDEX t1.a = t0.1
          IF (NOT (t0.0,t1.1) ∈ P_0)
           PROJECT (t0.0, t1.1) INTO @new_P_0
     END_DEBUG
    END PARALLEL
    EXIT (@new_P_0 = ∅)
    QUERY
     FOR t0 IN @new_P_0
      PROJECT (t0.0, t0.1) INTO P_0
    SWAP (@delta_P_0, @new_P_0)
    CLEAR @new_P_0
   END LOOP
   CLEAR @delta_P_0
   CLEAR @new_P_0
   CLEAR E_0
  END_STRATUM 9

       PROJECT (t0.0, t0.1) INTO P

     PROJECT (t0.0, t0.1) INTO @delta_P
   LOOP
    PARALLEL
     BEGIN_DEBUG "P(a,b) :- \n   P(a,x),\n   P(x,b).\nin file /home/default/souffle/experiments/NR-splitjoin-8-first.dl [45:1-45:26]"
      QUERY
       IF ((NOT (@delta_P = ∅)) AND (NOT (P = ∅)))
        FOR t0 IN @delta_P
         FOR t1 IN P ON INDEX t1.a = t0.1
          IF ((NOT (t0.1,t1.1) ∈ @delta_P) AND (NOT (t0.0,t1.1) ∈ P))
           PROJECT (t0.0, t1.1) INTO @new_P
     END_DEBUG
     BEGIN_DEBUG "P(a,b) :- \n   P(a,x),\n   P(x,b).\nin file /home/default/souffle/experiments/NR-splitjoin-8-first.dl [45:1-45:26]"
      QUERY
       IF ((NOT (P = ∅)) AND (NOT (@delta_P = ∅)))
        FOR t0 IN P
         FOR t1 IN @delta_P ON INDEX t1.a = t0.1
          IF (NOT (t0.0,t1.1) ∈ P)
           PROJECT (t0.0, t1.1) INTO @new_P
     END_DEBUG
    END PARALLEL
    EXIT (@new_P = ∅)
    QUERY
     FOR t0 IN @new_P
      PROJECT (t0.0, t0.1) INTO P
    SWAP (@delta_P, @new_P)
    CLEAR @new_P
   END LOOP
   CLEAR @delta_P
   CLEAR @new_P
   STORE DATA FOR P TO {{{"","default"},{"IO","file"},{"append","false"},{"attributeNames","a\tb"},{"directory","csv"},{"extension",".csv"},{"filename","csv/P.csv"},{"location","output-dir"},{"name","P"},{"stratum","slave"}}}

    QUERY
     IF (NOT (E_0 = ∅))

       PROJECT (t0.0, t0.1) INTO P_0
   END_DEBUG
   QUERY
    FOR t0 IN P_0
     PROJECT (t0.0, t0.1) INTO @delta_P_0
   LOOP
    PARALLEL
     BEGIN_DEBUG "P_0(a,b) :- \n   P_0(a,x),\n   P_0(x,b).\nin file /home/default/souffle/experiments/NR-splitjoin-8-first.dl [8:23-8:54]"
      QUERY
       IF ((NOT (@delta_P_0 = ∅)) AND (NOT (P_0 = ∅)))
        FOR t0 IN @delta_P_0
         FOR t1 IN P_0 ON INDEX t1.a = t0.1
          IF ((NOT (t0.1,t1.1) ∈ @delta_P_0) AND (NOT (t0.0,t1.1) ∈ P_0))
           PROJECT (t0.0, t1.1) INTO @new_P_0
     END_DEBUG
     BEGIN_DEBUG "P_0(a,b) :- \n   P_0(a,x),\n   P_0(x,b).\nin file /home/default/souffle/experiments/NR-splitjoin-8-first.dl [8:23-8:54]"

          IF (NOT (t0.0,t1.1) ∈ P_0)
           PROJECT (t0.0, t1.1) INTO @new_P_0
     END_DEBUG
    END PARALLEL
    EXIT (@new_P_0 = ∅)
    QUERY
     FOR t0 IN @new_P_0
      PROJECT (t0.0, t0.1) INTO P_0
    SWAP (@delta_P_0, @new_P_0)
    CLEAR @new_P_0
   END LOOP
   CLEAR @delta_P_0
   CLEAR @new_P_0
   CLEAR E_0

     END_DEBUG
    END PARALLEL
    EXIT (@new_P = ∅)
    QUERY
     FOR t0 IN @new_P
      PROJECT (t0.0, t0.1) INTO P
    SWAP (@delta_P, @new_P)
    CLEAR @new_P
   END LOOP
   CLEAR @delta_P
   CLEAR @new_P
   STORE DATA FOR P TO {{{"","default"},{"IO","file"},{"append","false"},{"attributeNames","a\tb"},{"directory","csv"},{"extension",".csv"},{"filename","csv/P.csv"},{"location","output-dir"},{"name","P"},{"stratum","slave"}}}
   CLEAR P
   CLEAR P_0
   CLEAR P_1
   CLEAR P_2
   CLEAR P_3
   CLEAR P_4
   CLEAR P_5
   CLEAR P_6
   CLEAR P_7
  END_STRATUM 17
 END MAIN
END PROGRAM
